A stately conference room on the top floor of Fallujah's headquarters in Miertenga territory.

From the window, I could see the vast industrial area and the mountains of the Crescent region spreading out in the distance.

Fallujah CEO Michael Gabrieli sits at one end of the table.
He was carefully observing the woman sitting in the seat across from him.

President of Miertenga, Marina Bobin.
Late 30s, black hair tied tightly back.
Dressed in a formal military-like suit,
A leader known for his ruthlessness.

Marina spoke in a quiet but strong voice.

“CEO Michael.
I'll say it straight to the point.
I would like to propose the creation of a government agency that would unify the entire Crescent region.
The current state of division among nations is inefficient and dangerous.
"It's creating the ground for threats like Silver Venom to rise."

Michael pushed up his silver-rimmed glasses,
I responded calmly.

"It's an interesting proposal.
However, a unified government would greatly limit the sovereignty of each nation.
Vermilion, Blue Rose, SUDOM...
I don't think everyone will accept it easily."

Marina smiled,
A hologram was projected onto the table.
A map of the entire Crescent region,
Organizational chart of the unified government plan.

"That's why we need Fallujah's cooperation.
Your economic strength, technological strength, and information network――
With these, Miertenga can stand at the center of the unification process.
I can demonstrate my presence overwhelmingly.
In the future, Miertenga could take control of Crescent's economic center.''

Michael looked at the map.
I thought about it for a while.

On the screen is the name of Yonic, the supreme commander of the Blue Rose government.

I thought about it for a while.

At that time,
Michael's communicator vibrated.

On the screen is the name of Yonic, the supreme commander of the Blue Rose government.

Michael lightly declines Marina and answers the call.

《CEO Michael!
　It's a big deal!

The one who captured it and released all the victims was...
It's a mysterious duo of heroes led by Fiona!

It was a night when a little bit of light returned.

A stately conference room on the top floor of Fallujah's headquarters in Miertenga territory.

From the window, I could see the vast industrial area and the mountains of the Crescent region spreading out in the distance.

Fallujah CEO Michael Gabrieli sits at one end of the table.
He was carefully observing the woman sitting in the seat across from him.

President of Miertenga, Marina Bobin.
Late 30s, black hair tied tightly back.
Dressed in a formal military-like suit,
A leader known for his ruthlessness.

Marina spoke in a quiet but strong voice.

“CEO Michael.
I'll say it straight to the point.
I would like to propose the creation of a government agency that would unify the entire Crescent region.
The current state of division among nations is inefficient and dangerous.
"It's creating the ground for threats like Silver Venom to rise."

Michael pushed up his silver-rimmed glasses,
I responded calmly.

"It's an interesting proposal.
However, a unified government would greatly limit the sovereignty of each nation.
Vermilion, Blue Rose, SUDOM...
I don't think everyone will accept it easily."

Marina smiled,
A hologram was projected onto the table.
A map of the entire Crescent region,
Organizational chart of the unified government plan.

"That's why we need Fallujah's cooperation.
Your economic strength, technological strength, and information network――
With these, Miertenga can stand at the center of the unification process.
I can demonstrate my presence overwhelmingly.
In the future, Miertenga could take control of Crescent's economic center.''

Michael looked at the map.
I thought about it for a while.

At that time,
Michael's communicator vibrated.

On the screen is the name of Yonic, the supreme commander of the Blue Rose government.

Michael lightly declines Marina and answers the call.

《CEO Michael!
　It's a big deal!
The long-standing kidnapping case of a woman in an underground shopping mall has suddenly been solved!
The culprit is "Last Man", a remnant of Silver Venom.
The one who captured it and released all the victims was...
It's a mysterious duo of heroes led by Fiona!

I really have nothing but gratitude!
The pride of Fallujah! 》

Michael was speechless for a moment.

“…Fiona?
She should have returned to Miertenga, but...
What are you doing in the underground mall...? ”

Michael, who had not been following Fiona's movements at all,
I could only be astonished.

Marina smiled curiously,
I asked Michael after he hung up.

“Any good news?”

Michael smiled bitterly,
“It seems our COO has become a hero again without permission...”
I just answered.

--Meanwhile, Witvia is the capital of Charlotte Scarlet Range (SS Range).

Ike Lopez, head of government of SS Range,

A young and ambitious leader

Sheron shook her gray hair,
I answered quietly.

“It’s true.
We are already following some traces.
If you cooperate, we can eliminate it quickly."

Gabby flips out her high-collared coat,
He added with a light laugh.

“In addition, the technical capabilities of the SS range are attractive.
I would like to deepen our cooperative relationship.”

Ike nodded with satisfaction.

“Good.
"Welcome, Bogdas."

I will do my best to contribute.”

``Now then, I would like to ask the two advisors immediately.

What do you think about the creation of the Crescent Greater Regional Unification Government? ”

``President Marina's proposal is interesting, but
As Vermilion, we need to secure the right to speak as much as possible.''

"As the second-largest economy, there is no point unless we can take the lead.
The first place SS range has an advantage in technology, but
"Our military power and population are overwhelming."

“The third-ranked Iron Syndicate is military-oriented,
4th place Crosevia relies on resources,
5th place Miertenga has the economic power of Fallujah, but...
The distribution of voting rights in a unified government should be decided based on a composite index of economic size and military power."

The high-ranking officials continued to have heated discussions,
We asked Miyushari and Aina for their opinions.

Miyushari smiled quietly,
He answered while lightly pressing his crotch.

"I think a unified government would be effective against threats like Silver Venom and X.
However, Vermilion's right to speak should certainly be strongly secured.
If we take advantage of our strengths as the second largest economy,
There is a high possibility that you will be able to take on a substantial leadership role.''

Aina also nodded seriously.

“I agree from a military perspective.
Vermilion's regular army is top class in both quality and quantity.
If a unified government is established,
This should be the center of defense."

Azazel nodded with satisfaction at the two's opinions,
He turned to the dignitaries.

``I also heard the opinions of the two advisors.
In Vermilion's unified government concept,
Never leave behind.
Let's proceed in a way where we take the lead.''

A strong applause echoed in the reception room.

Miyushari and Aina are
While feeling Vermilion's male-dominated atmosphere,
In a new stage role,
He was quietly burning with fighting spirit.

The future of the Crescent region is
It was starting to move little by little.
